</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Incidental_music&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Incidental music</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="31 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_voice&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the voice</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_mixed_chorus&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring mixed chorus</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Peer Gynt
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Grieg,_Edvard" title="Category:Grieg, Edvard">Grieg, Edvard</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.23
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IEG 79
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 acts
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act I
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prelude: At the Wedding (I brudlaupsgarden)
</dd><dd>2. Norwegian Bridal Procession in passing (Brudefylgjet dreg forbi)
</dd><dd>3. Halling &amp; Springar (Halling og Springdans)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act II
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>4. Prelude: The Abduction of the Bride / Peer and Ingrid (Bruderovet / Ingrids klage)
</dd><dd>5. Peer Gynt and the Herd-Girls (Peer Gynt og seterjentene)
</dd><dd>6. Peer Gynt and the Woman in Green (Peer Gynt og den grønkledde)
</dd><dd>7. Great folk may be known by the mounts... (På ridestellet skal storfolk kjennast)
</dd><dd>8. In the Hall of the Mountain King (I Dovregubbens hall)
</dd><dd>9. Dance of the Mountain King's Daughter (Dans av Dovregubbens dotter)
</dd><dd>10. Peer Gynt hunted by the trolls (Peer Gynt jagast av troll)
</dd><dd>11. Peer Gynt and the Boyg (Peer Gynt og Bøygen)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act III
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>12. Prelude: Deep Inside the Pine Forest
</dd><dd>13. Solveig's Song
</dd><dd>14. The Death of Åse (Åses daud)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act IV
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>15. Prelude: Morning Mood (Morgonstemning)
</dd><dd>16. The Thief and the Receiver (Tjuven og heilaren)
</dd><dd>17. Arabian Dance (Arabisk dans)
</dd><dd>18. Anitra's Dance (Anitras dans)
</dd><dd>19. Peer Gynt's Serenade (Peer Gynts serenade)
</dd><dd>20. Peer Gynt and Anitra (Peer og Anitra)
</dd><dd>21. Solveig's Song (Solveigs sang)
</dd><dd>22. Peer Gynt at the Statue of Memnon (Peer Gynt ved Memnonstøtten)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act V
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>23. Prelude: Peer Gynt's Homecoming. Stormy Evening on the Sea<br />(Peer Gynts heimfart. Stormfull aften ved kysten)
</dd><dd>24. Shipwreck (Skipsforliset)
</dd><dd>25. Solveig sings in the hut (Solveig syngjer i hytta)
</dd><dd>26. Night Scene (Nattscene)
</dd><dd>27. Whitsun Hymn (Pinsesalme)
</dd><dd>28. Solveig's Cradle Song (Solveigs vuggevise)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1875
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1876-02-24 in Christiania
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1877
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Ibsen,_Henrik" title="Category:Ibsen, Henrik">Henrik Ibsen</a>&#160;(1828-1906)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>Norwegian
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Peer Gynt (tenor)<br />Solveig (soprano)<br />Anitra (mezzo-soprano)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Chorus</i>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i>
<dl><dd>piccolo, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets (A), 2 bassoons<br />4 horns (E), 2 trumpets (E), 3 trombones, tuba<br />timpani, cymbals, bass drum, triangle, harp, hardanger fiddle (ad lib.), strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
